      function addToCart(addUrl){
    $.ajax({
      url: "https://www.fantasygrounds.com/store/addtocartmenuAB.php" + addUrl,
      type: 'GET',

     })
     .done(function(response ) {
         //response - this is the response from the server

        //location.reload();       
        $('#ShoppingCartMenu').html(response);
        alert("Shopping Cart Updated");
        
     });
 }

<script>
// Data passed from PHP
var saleStartDate = new Date("").getTime();
var saleEndDate = new Date("").getTime();
var saleDiscount = ;
var majorSale = ;
var originalPrice = ;
var newPrice = originalPrice * (1 - saleDiscount); 
var now = new Date().getTime();

// Add the sale indicator for licenses
var discountDiv = document.getElementById("license-sale-callout");
if (now >= saleStartDate && now <= saleEndDate) {
	if (discountDiv) {
		var percentOff  = Math.round(saleDiscount * 100);
		
		discountDiv.innerHTML = percentOff  + "% OFF";
		discountDiv.classList.remove("hidden");
	}
} else {
	discountDiv.classList.add("hidden");
}

// Add the correct price
var licensePrice = document.getElementById("licensePrice");
if (now >= saleStartDate && now <= saleEndDate) {
	if (licensePrice) {
		licensePrice.innerText = newPrice.toFixed(2);
	}
}

// Add the timer that tells when the sale ends
var x = setInterval(function() {
  var now = new Date().getTime();
  var targetDiv = document.getElementById("sale-timer-countdown");

  if (now >= saleStartDate && now <= saleEndDate) {
	targetDiv.classList.remove("hidden");
    var distance = saleEndDate - now;
    
    var days = Math.floor(distance / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
    var hours = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)) / (1000 * 60 * 60));
    var minutes = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60 * 60)) / (1000 * 60));
    var seconds = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60)) / 1000);

    var percent = Math.round(saleDiscount * 100);
    
    var existingBanner = document.getElementById("sale-message");

    if (!existingBanner && targetDiv) {
      var salePara = document.createElement("p");
      salePara.id = "sale-message";
	  salePara.innerHTML = "ENDS in <span id='sale-countdown'></span>";
	  targetDiv.insertBefore(salePara, targetDiv.firstChild);
    }

    var countdownSpan = document.getElementById("sale-countdown");
    if (countdownSpan) {
      countdownSpan.innerText = days + "d " + hours + "h " + minutes + "m " + seconds + "s";
    }

  } else {
	targetDiv.classList.add("hidden");
    clearInterval(x);
    var banner = document.getElementById("sale-message");
    if (banner) {
      banner.remove();
    }
  }
}, 1000);
</script>

<!-- Add to Cart Code -->

<script type="text/javascript">
    
      function addToCart(addUrl){
    $.ajax({
      url: "https://www.fantasygrounds.com/store/addtocartmenuAB.php" + addUrl,
      type: 'GET',

     })
     .done(function(response ) {
         //response - this is the response from the server
        // Refresh Cart indicator here 
        //location.reload();       
        $('#ShoppingCartMenu').html(response);
        alert("Shopping Cart Updated");
        
     });
 }

</script>

<script>
// Data passed from PHP
var saleStartDate = new Date("").getTime();
var saleEndDate = new Date("").getTime();
var saleDiscount = ;
var majorSale = ;
var originalPrice = ;
var newPrice = originalPrice * (1 - saleDiscount); 
var now = new Date().getTime();

// Add the sale indicator for licenses
var discountDiv = document.getElementById("license-sale-callout");
if (now >= saleStartDate && now <= saleEndDate) {
	if (discountDiv) {
		var percentOff  = Math.round(saleDiscount * 100);
		
		discountDiv.innerHTML = percentOff  + "% OFF";
		discountDiv.classList.remove("hidden");
	}
} else {
	discountDiv.classList.add("hidden");
}

// Add the correct price
var licensePrice = document.getElementById("licensePrice");
if (now >= saleStartDate && now <= saleEndDate) {
	if (licensePrice) {
		licensePrice.innerText = newPrice.toFixed(2);
	}
}

// Add the timer that tells when the sale ends
var x = setInterval(function() {
  var now = new Date().getTime();
  var targetDiv = document.getElementById("sale-timer-countdown");

  if (now >= saleStartDate && now <= saleEndDate) {
	targetDiv.classList.remove("hidden");
    var distance = saleEndDate - now;
    
    var days = Math.floor(distance / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
    var hours = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)) / (1000 * 60 * 60));
    var minutes = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60 * 60)) / (1000 * 60));
    var seconds = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60)) / 1000);

    var percent = Math.round(saleDiscount * 100);
    
    var existingBanner = document.getElementById("sale-message");

    if (!existingBanner && targetDiv) {
      var salePara = document.createElement("p");
      salePara.id = "sale-message";
	  salePara.innerHTML = "ENDS in <span id='sale-countdown'></span>";
	  targetDiv.insertBefore(salePara, targetDiv.firstChild);
    }

    var countdownSpan = document.getElementById("sale-countdown");
    if (countdownSpan) {
      countdownSpan.innerText = days + "d " + hours + "h " + minutes + "m " + seconds + "s";
    }

  } else {
	targetDiv.classList.add("hidden");
    clearInterval(x);
    var banner = document.getElementById("sale-message");
    if (banner) {
      banner.remove();
    }
  }
}, 1000);
</script>

<script>
// Data passed from PHP
var saleStartDate = new Date("").getTime();
var saleEndDate = new Date("").getTime();
var saleDiscount = ;
var majorSale = ;
var originalPrice = ;
var newPrice = originalPrice * (1 - saleDiscount); 
var now = new Date().getTime();

// Add the sale indicator for licenses
var discountDiv = document.getElementById("license-sale-callout");
if (now >= saleStartDate && now <= saleEndDate) {
	if (discountDiv) {
		var percentOff  = Math.round(saleDiscount * 100);
		
		discountDiv.innerHTML = percentOff  + "% OFF";
		discountDiv.classList.remove("hidden");
	}
} else {
	discountDiv.classList.add("hidden");
}

// Add the correct price
var licensePrice = document.getElementById("licensePrice");
if (now >= saleStartDate && now <= saleEndDate) {
	if (licensePrice) {
		licensePrice.innerText = newPrice.toFixed(2);
	}
}

// Add the timer that tells when the sale ends
var x = setInterval(function() {
  var now = new Date().getTime();
  var targetDiv = document.getElementById("sale-timer-countdown");

  if (now >= saleStartDate && now <= saleEndDate) {
	targetDiv.classList.remove("hidden");
    var distance = saleEndDate - now;
    
    var days = Math.floor(distance / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
    var hours = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)) / (1000 * 60 * 60));
    var minutes = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60 * 60)) / (1000 * 60));
    var seconds = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60)) / 1000);

    var percent = Math.round(saleDiscount * 100);
    
    var existingBanner = document.getElementById("sale-message");

    if (!existingBanner && targetDiv) {
      var salePara = document.createElement("p");
      salePara.id = "sale-message";
	  salePara.innerHTML = "ENDS in <span id='sale-countdown'></span>";
	  targetDiv.insertBefore(salePara, targetDiv.firstChild);
    }

    var countdownSpan = document.getElementById("sale-countdown");
    if (countdownSpan) {
      countdownSpan.innerText = days + "d " + hours + "h " + minutes + "m " + seconds + "s";
    }

  } else {
	targetDiv.classList.add("hidden");
    clearInterval(x);
    var banner = document.getElementById("sale-message");
    if (banner) {
      banner.remove();
    }
  }
}, 1000);
</script>

<script>
// Data passed from PHP
var saleStartDate = new Date("").getTime();
var saleEndDate = new Date("").getTime();
var saleDiscount = ;
var majorSale = ;
var originalPrice = ;
var newPrice = originalPrice * (1 - saleDiscount); 
var now = new Date().getTime();

// Add the sale indicator for licenses
var discountDiv = document.getElementById("license-sale-callout");
if (now >= saleStartDate && now <= saleEndDate) {
	if (discountDiv) {
		var percentOff  = Math.round(saleDiscount * 100);
		
		discountDiv.innerHTML = percentOff  + "% OFF";
		discountDiv.classList.remove("hidden");
	}
} else {
	discountDiv.classList.add("hidden");
}

// Add the correct price
var licensePrice = document.getElementById("licensePrice");
if (now >= saleStartDate && now <= saleEndDate) {
	if (licensePrice) {
		licensePrice.innerText = newPrice.toFixed(2);
	}
}

// Add the timer that tells when the sale ends
var x = setInterval(function() {
  var now = new Date().getTime();
  var targetDiv = document.getElementById("sale-timer-countdown");

  if (now >= saleStartDate && now <= saleEndDate) {
	targetDiv.classList.remove("hidden");
    var distance = saleEndDate - now;
    
    var days = Math.floor(distance / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
    var hours = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)) / (1000 * 60 * 60));
    var minutes = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60 * 60)) / (1000 * 60));
    var seconds = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60)) / 1000);

    var percent = Math.round(saleDiscount * 100);
    
    var existingBanner = document.getElementById("sale-message");

    if (!existingBanner && targetDiv) {
      var salePara = document.createElement("p");
      salePara.id = "sale-message";
	  salePara.innerHTML = "ENDS in <span id='sale-countdown'></span>";
	  targetDiv.insertBefore(salePara, targetDiv.firstChild);
    }

    var countdownSpan = document.getElementById("sale-countdown");
    if (countdownSpan) {
      countdownSpan.innerText = days + "d " + hours + "h " + minutes + "m " + seconds + "s";
    }

  } else {
	targetDiv.classList.add("hidden");
    clearInterval(x);
    var banner = document.getElementById("sale-message");
    if (banner) {
      banner.remove();
    }
  }
}, 1000);
</script>

<script>
// Data passed from PHP
var saleStartDate = new Date("").getTime();
var saleEndDate = new Date("").getTime();
var saleDiscount = ;
var majorSale = ;
var originalPrice = ;
var newPrice = originalPrice * (1 - saleDiscount); 
var now = new Date().getTime();

// Add the sale indicator for licenses
var discountDiv = document.getElementById("license-sale-callout");
if (now >= saleStartDate && now <= saleEndDate) {
	if (discountDiv) {
		var percentOff  = Math.round(saleDiscount * 100);
		
		discountDiv.innerHTML = percentOff  + "% OFF";
		discountDiv.classList.remove("hidden");
	}
} else {
	discountDiv.classList.add("hidden");
}

// Add the correct price
var licensePrice = document.getElementById("licensePrice");
if (now >= saleStartDate && now <= saleEndDate) {
	if (licensePrice) {
		licensePrice.innerText = newPrice.toFixed(2);
	}
}

// Add the timer that tells when the sale ends
var x = setInterval(function() {
  var now = new Date().getTime();
  var targetDiv = document.getElementById("sale-timer-countdown");

  if (now >= saleStartDate && now <= saleEndDate) {
	targetDiv.classList.remove("hidden");
    var distance = saleEndDate - now;
    
    var days = Math.floor(distance / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
    var hours = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)) / (1000 * 60 * 60));
    var minutes = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60 * 60)) / (1000 * 60));
    var seconds = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60)) / 1000);

    var percent = Math.round(saleDiscount * 100);
    
    var existingBanner = document.getElementById("sale-message");

    if (!existingBanner && targetDiv) {
      var salePara = document.createElement("p");
      salePara.id = "sale-message";
	  salePara.innerHTML = "ENDS in <span id='sale-countdown'></span>";
	  targetDiv.insertBefore(salePara, targetDiv.firstChild);
    }

    var countdownSpan = document.getElementById("sale-countdown");
    if (countdownSpan) {
      countdownSpan.innerText = days + "d " + hours + "h " + minutes + "m " + seconds + "s";
    }

  } else {
	targetDiv.classList.add("hidden");
    clearInterval(x);
    var banner = document.getElementById("sale-message");
    if (banner) {
      banner.remove();
    }
  }
}, 1000);
</script>
